<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/saveOrUpdateDep',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_search").click();//刷新
layer.close($("#index_q").val());
}
});
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist');
//var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP￾formlist");
// $("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_search").click(function(){
// easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist');
// });
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
var pV = layui.$("#Q_WORKSTUDY_PLAN_UID").val();
var pT = layui.$("#Q_WORKSTUDY_PLAN_TYPE").val();
var data1 = {planUid:pV};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsdep/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP','easyajax/job
sPlanManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#index_q").val(d.index);
layui.$("#input_workstudy_college_id").attr("src","T#BASE_SYS_COLLEGE :COLLEGE_CODE :COLL
EGE_NAME :DATA_STATUS=1 AND COLLEGE_TYPE='"+pT+"' ORDER BY COLLEGE_NAME ASC");
layui.easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP');
if(pT=='1'){
$("#title-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").html("学院");
layui.$("#input_job_nums_id").removeAttr("lay-verify");
layui.$("#input_all_amounts_id").attr("lay-verify","required");
$("#ALL_AMOUNTS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").show();
$("#JOB_NUMS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").hide()
}else{
layui.$("#input_all_amounts_id").removeAttr("lay-verify");
layui.$("#input_job_nums_id").attr("lay-verify","required");
$("#title-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").html("部门");
$("#JOB_NUMS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").show()
$("#ALL_AMOUNTS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").hide();
}
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {depUid:data.DEP_UID,dataStatus:'-1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/updateDepStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {depUid:data.DEP_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsdep/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP','easyajax/job
sPlanManage/getDepMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#index_q").val(d.index);
layui.$("#input_workstudy_college_id").attr("defaultValue",d.COLLEGE_CODE);
layui.$("#input_workstudy_college_id").attr("src","T#BASE_SYS_COLLEGE :COLLEGE_CODE :
COLLEGE_NAME :DATA_STATUS=1 AND COLLEGE_TYPE='"+d.PLAN_TYPE+"' ORDER BY
COLLEGE_NAME ASC");
layui.easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP')
if(d.PLAN_TYPE=='1'){
$("#title-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").html("学院");
layui.$("#input_job_nums_id").removeAttr("lay-verify");
layui.$("#input_all_amounts_id").attr("lay-verify","required");
$("#ALL_AMOUNTS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").show();
$("#JOB_NUMS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").hide()
}else{
layui.$("#input_all_amounts_id").removeAttr("lay-verify");
layui.$("#input_job_nums_id").attr("lay-verify","required");
$("#title-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").html("部门");
$("#JOB_NUMS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").show()
$("#ALL_AMOUNTS-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP").hide();
}
});
} else if(obj.event === 'down'){
layer.confirm("确定注销该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {depUid:data.DEP_UID,dataStatus:'0'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/updateDepStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'publish'){
layer.confirm("确定启用该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {depUid:data.DEP_UID,dataStatus:'1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {depUid:data.DEP_UID};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsdep/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP','easyajax/job
sPlanManage/getDepMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','laytpl','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,laytpl = layui.laytpl ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
//初始化上传控件界面
easyUpload.initClickFileUploadHtml(0,function successFun(res){
var data={num:0,title:'岗位雇佣信息上传'};
layui.laytpl(res.innerHTML).render(data, function(html){
document.getElementById('uploadEmployFileId0').innerHTML = html;
});
});
//初始化上传控件
easyUpload.initClickFileUpload(0,'easyfile/jobsEmployManage/importExcel',function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#down_mes_0").html(res.resultinfo);
$("#imp_retfilepath_0").val(res.retfilepath);
$("#resultinfoId_0").show();
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
//导出结果下载
$("#downResButton0").click(function(){
var f = $("#imp_retfilepath_0").val();
if(f!=null && f!=''){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downResult?fileName=' +f,'impgwgy_result');
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error',"下载文件不存在！");
}
});
$("#downButton").click(function(){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downTemplate?fileNam
e=workstudy/imp_gwgy.xlsx','imp_gwgy');
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','easybankutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easybankutils=layui.easybankutils;
//日期控件绑定
easyutils.renderDate('layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY');
var selectsS=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsInfo('#INPUT_JOBSINFO_SELID_SETUP',selectsS,function
successFun(o,d){
var seleV = o.values.join(",");
layui.$("#INPUT_JOBSINFO_SELVALUE_SETUP").val(seleV);
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/jobsEmployManage/saveOrUpdate',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
$("#btn_search_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY").click(function(){
var stuData = layui.$("#SEARCH_STU_DATA_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY").val();
if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
var data1 = {SEARCH_STU_DATA:stuData};
easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/studentInfoManage/getStuInfoMap',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
var successData=res.data;
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY",successData);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_STU_NO").val(successData.STU_STU_NO);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_TEL_NUM").val(successData.STU_TEL_NUM);
if(successData.BANK_NAME && successData.BANK_NAME=='BOC'){//中
国银行
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_BANK_CODE").val(successData.STU_BANK_CODE);
}
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_BANK_CODE").val(successData.STU_BANK_CODE);
var dicObj=$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_BANK_NAME");
dicObj.attr("defaultValue",successData.STU_BANK_NAME);
dicObj.html('');
easyutils.reloadSelectDic(dicObj);
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY');
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
return false;
}
});
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号/身份证号数据！');
return false;
}
});
});
function verifyBankFun(){
var bankCode = layui.$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_BANK_CODE").val();
var v = layui.easybankutils.verifyBankCardNumber(bankCode);
if(!v){
layui.$("#WORKSTUDY_BANK_CODE_ID_mes").html("输入的银行卡号格式不对，请核
对");
}
//var b = layui.easybankutils.bankCardAttribution(bankCode);
}
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
//日期控件绑定
easyutils.renderDate('layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY');
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.dataStatus='0';
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/jobsEmployManage/updateStatus',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsInfo('#Q_WORK_EMPLOY_SELID_JOBS',selects1,function
empWorkCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_WORK_EMPLOY_SELVALUE_JOBS").val(o.values.join(","));
});//岗位计划、部门、岗位
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_
EMPLOY-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click(function(){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_ISE").val("0");
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-formlist');
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsemploy/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY',null, null,null);
break;
case 'stu_import':
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 岗 位 雇 佣 信 息 导 入
",'70%','95%','workstudy/jobsemploy/employ_import','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMP
LOY', null, function renderDoneFun(d){
});
break;
case 'batchlig':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="",isCon=true;
var checkNames = [],checkNos=[];
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.EMPLOY_UID+",";
checkNames.push(item.STU_STU_NAME);
checkNos.push(item.STU_NO);
if(item.EMPLOY_STATUS=='0'){
layer.msg('所选择数据包括已离岗的数据，请核实之后再进行操作！');
isCon=false;
}
});
if(isCon){
var data1 = {checkNames:checkNames,checkNos:checkNos};
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 批 量 离 岗
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsemploy/leave_input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY
',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_EMPLOY_UIDS").val(checkUids);
});
}
break;
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！
", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_ISE").val("1");
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/jobsEmployManage/query'," 岗 位 雇 佣
信息.xlsx",dataP);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {employUid:data.EMPLOY_UID};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsEmployManage/delete',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {employUid:data.EMPLOY_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsemploy/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY','easy
ajax/jobsEmployManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
layui.$("#INPUT_JOBSINFO_SELVALUE_SETUP").val(d.PLAN_UID+","+d.DEP_UID+","+d.JOB_ UID);
var selectsS=[d.PLAN_UID,d.DEP_UID,d.JOB_UID];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsInfo('#INPUT_JOBSINFO_SELID_SETUP',selectsS,function
successFun(o,d){
var seleV = o.values.join(",");
layui.$("#INPUT_JOBSINFO_SELVALUE_SETUP").val(seleV);
});
$("#div_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY").hide();
console.log(d);
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY",d);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'down'){
layer.confirm("确定对该生进行离岗操作？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {employUid:data.EMPLOY_UID,dataStatus:'0'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsEmployManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
var checkUids=data.EMPLOY_UID;
var checkNames = [],checkNos=[];
checkNames.push(data.STU_STU_NAME);
checkNos.push(data.STU_NO);
var data1 = {checkNames:checkNames,checkNos:checkNos};
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 离 岗
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsemploy/leave_input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY
',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_EMPLOY_UIDS").val(checkUids);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'publish'){
layer.confirm("确定对该生进行上岗操作？上岗将覆盖之前的离岗日期，此操作不能
撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {employUids:data.EMPLOY_UID,dataStatus:'1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsEmployManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {employUid:data.EMPLOY_UID,isView:'1'};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsemploy/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY','easy
ajax/jobsEmployManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
//$('#IMG_COVER').attr('src', d.IMG_COVER);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'toSalary'){
var title = data.STU_STU_NAME +"["+data.STU_NO+"]"+"在【"+data.JOB_NAME+"】
的工资条";
easyutils.popupViewWindow(title,'90%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/from_list','layadmin-WORKS
TUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist',null,null,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_QSTU_NO").val(data.STU_NO);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_QJOB_UID").val(data.JOB_UID);
var
tableSalaryObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_J
OBS_FSALARY-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableSalaryObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist');
});
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
var selectsS=[null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsPlan('#INPUT_JOBSPLAN_SELID_SETUP',selectsS,function
successFun(o,d){
var seleV = o.values.join(",");
layui.$("#INPUT_JOBSPLAN_SELVALUE_SETUP").val(seleV);
});//岗位计划及岗位部门学院选择
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/jobsInfoManage/saveOrUpdate',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
var selects1=[null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsPlan('#Q_WORK_INFO_SELID_JOBS',selects1,function
jobInfoCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_WORK_INFO_SELVALUE_JOBS").val(o.values.join(","));
});//岗位计划、部门、岗位
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INF
O-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_search").click(function(){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_ISE").val("0");
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-formlist');
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsinfo/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO',null,null,nul
l);
break;
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！
", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_ISE").val("1");
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyajax/jobsInfoManage/query'," 岗 位 信
息.xlsx",dataP);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {jobUid:data.JOB_UID,dataStatus:'-1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsInfoManage/updateStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {jobUid:data.JOB_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsinfo/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO','easyajax/jo
bsInfoManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
var selectsS=[d.PLAN_UID,d.DEP_UID];
layui.$("#INPUT_JOBSPLAN_SELVALUE_SETUP").val(d.PLAN_UID+","+d.DEP_UID);
layui.easyutils.selectJobsPlan('#INPUT_JOBSPLAN_SELID_SETUP',selectsS,function
successFun(o,d){
var seleV = o.values.join(",");
layui.$("#INPUT_JOBSPLAN_SELVALUE_SETUP").val(seleV);
});//岗位计划及岗位部门学院选择
});
} else if(obj.event === 'down'){
layer.confirm("确定注销该信息？注销后此岗位信息不能被使用，此操作不能撤销！
", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {jobUid:data.JOB_UID,dataStatus:'0'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsInfoManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'publish'){
layer.confirm("确定启用该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {jobUid:data.JOB_UID,dataStatus:'1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsInfoManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {jobUid:data.JOB_UID,isView:'1'};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobsinfo/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO','easyajax/jo
bsInfoManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script>
<style>
.layui-upload-img{width: 92px; height: 92px; margin: 0 10px 10px 0;}
</style>
<div class="layui-form layui-form-pane" lay-filter="layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO" >
<fieldset class="layui-elem-field ">
<legend style="color:#393D49;">岗位信息详情信息</legend>
<div class="layui-field-box">
<div class="layui-row layadmin-homepage-text-center">
<div class="layui-col-md12 layui-col-sm12 layui-col-xs12">
<p><strong>岗位名称：</strong> <mdall name="JOB_NAME"></mdall>
</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="layui-row layadmin-homepage-text-center">

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN-formlist');
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLA
N-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN-formlist');
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsplan/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN',null,null,nu
ll);
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {planUid:data.PLAN_UID,dataStatus:'-1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/updateStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {planUid:data.PLAN_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsplan/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN','easyajax/j
obsPlanManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
} else if(obj.event === 'down'){
layer.confirm("确定注销该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {planUid:data.PLAN_UID,dataStatus:'0'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'publish'){
layer.confirm("确定启用该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {planUid:data.PLAN_UID,dataStatus:'1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsPlanManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {planUid:data.PLAN_UID,isView:'1'};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobsplan/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN','easyajax/jo
bsPlanManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
} else if(obj.event === 'dep'){
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 岗 位 计 划 分 配
",'90%','95%','workstudy/jobsdep/list','layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist',null,null,functi
on renderDoneFun(d){
$("#Q_WORKSTUDY_PLAN_UID").val(data.PLAN_UID);
$("#Q_WORKSTUDY_PLAN_TYPE").val(data.PLAN_TYPE);
layui.$("#q_workstudy_college_id").attr("src","T#BASE_SYS_COLLEGE :COLLEGE_CODE :COLLEGE _NAME :DATA_STATUS=1 AND COLLEGE_TYPE='"+data.PLAN_TYPE+"' ORDER BY COLLEGE_NAME
ASC");
layui.easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist')
//区别隐藏 table 列
layui.$('table[lay-filter="easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP"]').find('thead>tr').each(function(i){
layui.$(this).children().each(function(ii){
var th = layui.$(this), itemData = th.attr('easy-data');
var obj = eval('(' + itemData + ')');
if(data.PLAN_TYPE=='1'){//学院
for(var p in obj){
if(obj[p] == 'JOB_NUMS'){
obj.hide = true;
break;
}
}
}
if(data.PLAN_TYPE=='2'){//部门
for(var p in obj){
if(obj[p] == 'ALL_AMOUNTS'){
obj.hide = true;
break;
}
}
}
th.attr("easy-data",JSON.stringify(obj));
});
});
var
tableDepObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_ DEP-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableDepObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP-formlist');
});
});
}else if(obj.event==='copyPlan'){
var data1 = {planUid:data.PLAN_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 复 制 岗 位 计 划
",'50%','90%','workstudy/jobsplan/copy_input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN',null, null,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#COPY_PLAN_UID").val(data.PLAN_UID);
$("#COPY_PLAN_NAME").val(data.PLAN_NAME)
});
}
});
});
</script>

<div class="layui-field-box">
<script type="text/html" template >
{{# if(d.params.depList){ }}
<div class="layui-row layadmin-homepage-text-center layui-form">

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist');
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist');
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
var stuNo = $("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_QSTU_NO").val();
var jobUid = $("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_QJOB_UID").val();
var data1 = {stuNo:stuNo,jobUid:jobUid};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'80%','90%','workstudy/jobssalary/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaj
ax/jobsSalaryManage/getInitMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#index_q").val(d.index);
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY",d);
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除该工资条吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsSalaryManage/delete',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaj
ax/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#index_q").val(d.index);
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY",d);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaja
x/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','laydate'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,laydate=layui.laydate;
easyutils.renderDateYear('layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY');
laydate.render({
elem: '#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_BEGIN_DATE' ,type: 'datetime' ,fontmat:"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"
});
laydate.render({
elem: '#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_END_DATE' ,type: 'datetime' ,fontmat:"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/jobsSalaryManage/saveOrUpdate',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_FSALARY_search").click();//刷新
layer.close($("#index_q").val());
}
});
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_close").click(function(){
layer.close($("#index_q").val());
});
});
function countSalaryFun(){
var amount = layui.$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_SALARY_AMOUNT").val();
var times = layui.$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_SALARY_TIMES").val();
if(amount!=null && amount!='' && times!=null && times!=''){
var zs = parseFloat(amount)*parseFloat(times);
layui.$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT").val(zs);
}
}
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload','laydate'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,laydate=layui.laydate
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
//年月范围
laydate.render({
elem: '#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_yearmonth' ,type: 'month' ,range: true
});
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsInfo('#Q_JOBS_SALARY_SELID_JOBS',selects1,function
salaryWorkCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_JOBS_SALARY_SELVALUE_JOBS").val(o.values.join(","));
});//岗位计划、部门、岗位
easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_S
ALARY-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_search").click(function(){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_ISE").val('0');
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'batchdel':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="",isCon=true;
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.SALARY_UID+",";
if(item.SALARY_STATUS=='2'){
layer.msg('所选择数据包括不可删除的数据，请核实之后再进行删除！');
isCon=false;
}
});
if(isCon){
layer.confirm('确定删除吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
var data1 = {salaryUid:checkUids};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsSalaryManage/delete',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
});
}
break;
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！
", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_ISE").val("1");
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/jobsSalaryManage/query',"岗位薪资结
算信息.xlsx",dataP);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
case 'batchsettle':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="",isCon=true;
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.SALARY_UID+",";
if(item.SALARY_STATUS!='1'){
layer.msg('所选择数据包括非待结算的数据，请核实之后再进行结算操作！
');
isCon=false;
}
});
if(isCon){
layer.confirm('确定对所选数据进行结算操作吗？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
var data1 = {salaryUids:checkUids};
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/jobsSalaryManage/batchSettle',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
});
}
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaj
ax/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY",d);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaja
x/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script>
<title>岗位薪资维护</title>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','laydate','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,laydate=layui.laydate
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
//年月范围
laydate.render({
elem: '#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_yearmonth' ,type: 'month' ,range: true
});
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectJobsInfo('#Q_JOBS_WSALARY_SELID_JOBS',selects1,function
salaryWorkCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_JOBS_WSALARY_SELVALUE_JOBS").val(o.values.join(","));
});//岗位计划、部门、岗位
easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS _WSALARY-formlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_search").click(function(){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISE").val('0');
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISET").val("0")
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'stu_import':
var successData = {YEAR_NUM:new Date().getFullYear()}
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 工 资 条 信 息 导 入
",'70%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/salary_import','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY
',successData,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
break;
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！
", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISE").val("1");
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISET").val("0")
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/jobsSalaryManage/query',"岗位薪资结
算信息.xlsx",dataP);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
case 'khb_export':
layer.confirm("确定根据检索条件导出勤工助学考核表吗？数据过大时，请使用查
询条件进行筛选过滤！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISE").val("1");
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISET").val("1")
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
//
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/jobsSalaryManage/query',"勤工助学考
核表.xlsx",dataP);
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/jobStuManage/queryStu',"学生勤工助
学汇总考核表.xlsx",dataP);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISE").val("0");
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY_ISET").val("0")
layer.close(index);
});
break;
case 'batchdel':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="",isCon=true;
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.SALARY_UID+",";
if(item.SALARY_STATUS=='2'){
layer.msg('所选择数据包括不可删除的数据，请核实之后再进行删除！
');
isCon=false;
}
});
if(isCon){
layer.confirm('确定删除吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
var data1 = {salaryUid:checkUids};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/jobsSalaryManage/delete',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
});
}
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_WSALARY)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'80%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/input','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaj
ax/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY",d);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {salaryUid:data.SALARY_UID};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaja
x/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script>
<div class="layui-form layui-form-pane" lay-filter="layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY"
style="padding: 20px 30px 0 0;">
<fieldset class="layui-elem-field ">
<legend style="color:#393D49;">岗位工资条信息导入</legend>
<div class="layui-field-box">
<div class="layui-form-item">
<label class="layui-form-label form-required">年份</label>
<div class="layui-input-inline">
<input type="text" name="YEAR_NUM" id="U_ONE_YEAR_NUM"
readonly="readonly" placeholder="年份" class="layui-input">
</div>
</div>
<div class="layui-form-item">

用】里面的报酬标准即可。</br>
3.导入系统的报酬标准和劳作总金额最终系统会根据模板中导入相
对应的岗位信息来自动计算，模板里面的报酬标准和劳作总金额不作为导入依据，显示出来
是方便老师过目。

<script>
layui.use(['form','laytpl','easyutils','laydate','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,laytpl = layui.laytpl ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload
,laydate=layui.laydate;
laydate.render({
elem: "#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM"
,type: 'year' ,value:'' ,change: function(value, date){ //日期被切换的回调
setValueFun();
}
});
//初始化上传控件界面
easyUpload.initClickFileUploadHtml(0,function successFun(res){
var data={num:0,title:'岗位工资条文件上传'};
layui.laytpl(res.innerHTML).render(data, function(html){
document.getElementById('uploadGwxzFileId0').innerHTML = html;
setValueFun();
});
});
//初始化上传控件
easyUpload.initClickFileUpload(0,'easyfile/jobsSalaryManage/importExcel',function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#down_mes_0").html(res.resultinfo);
$("#imp_retfilepath_0").val(res.retfilepath);
$("#resultinfoId_0").show();
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
//导出结果下载
$("#downResButton0").click(function(){
var f = $("#imp_retfilepath_0").val();
if(f!=null && f!=''){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downResult?fileName=' +f,'impgwxz_result');
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error',"下载文件不存在！");
}
});
$("#downButton").click(function(){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downTemplate?fileNam
e=workstudy/imp_gwxz.xlsx','imp_gwxz');
});
form.on('select(filter-MONTH_NUM)', function(data){
setValueFun();
});
});
function setValueFun(){
layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM").val());
layui.$("#U_TWO_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_MONTH_NUM").val());
}
</script>
<style>
.layui-upload-img{width: 92px; height: 92px; margin: 0 10px 10px 0;}
</style>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','laydate','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,laydate=layui.laydate
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
//年月范围
laydate.render({
elem: '#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_yearmonth' ,type: 'month' ,range: true
});
easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU',"layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-f
ormlist");
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_search").click(function(){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_ISE").val('0');
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
});
$("#btn_WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！
", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_ISE").val("1");
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/jobStuManage/queryAll'," 学 生 薪 资 报
表.xlsx",dataP);
$("#WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_STU)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {stuNo:data.STU_NO};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'60%','95%','workstudy/jobssalary/view','layuiadmin-form-WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY','easyaja
x/jobsSalaryManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script>

package com.easy.modules.workstudy.util;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.List;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.ISession;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.util.HashMap;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.db.DBQuery;
import com.easy.framework.constant.RoleTypeEnum;
import com.easy.modules.comm.util.EasydicDataUtil;
public class JobsDataUtils {
public static List<HashMap> getJobsPlanList(ISession session, String roleType, String optUid){
String planSql = "SELECT T.PLAN_UID, T.PLAN_NAME FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN T
WHERE T.PLAN_STATUS=? " ;
String jobsSql = " SELECT T.PLAN_UID AS SPECIALTY_CODE, T.DEP_UID AS CLASS_CODE, C.COLLEGE_NAME AS CLASS_NAME " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP T LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON
C.COLLEGE_CODE=T.COLLEGE_CODE WHERE T.DATA_STATUS=? ";
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
planSql +=" AND T.PLAN_TYPE ='1' ";
jobsSql +=" AND T.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
planSql +=" AND T.PLAN_TYPE ='2' ";
jobsSql +=" AND T.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
}
planSql +=" ORDER BY T.PLAN_NAME DESC ";
jobsSql +=" ORDER BY C.COLLEGE_NAME DESC ";
List<HashMap> dicList = null;
List<HashMap> stepList = DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, planSql, "1");
List<HashMap> gradeList = DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, jobsSql, "1");
if(stepList!=null&&stepList.size()>0) {
dicList=new ArrayList<HashMap>();
Iterator<HashMap> it = stepList.iterator();
while(it.hasNext()){
HashMap temMap = it.next();
HashMap collegeMap=new HashMap();
collegeMap.put("id", temMap.getString("PLAN_UID"));
collegeMap.put("name", temMap.getString("PLAN_NAME"));
List<HashMap> children =
EasydicDataUtil.getTwoChilrenList(collegeMap.getString("id"),gradeList);
if(children!=null && children.size()>0) {
collegeMap.put("children", children);
}
dicList.add(collegeMap);
}
//CacheHolderString.setData(CacheHolderString.DIC_LIST_JOBSPLAN, dicList);
}
return dicList;
}
public static List<HashMap> getJobsInfoList(ISession session, String roleType, String optUid){
List<HashMap> dicList = null;
String planSql = "SELECT T.PLAN_UID, T.PLAN_NAME FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN T
WHERE T.PLAN_STATUS=? " ;
String jobsSql = " SELECT T.PLAN_UID AS COLLEGE_CODE, T.DEP_UID AS
SPECIALTY_CODE, C.COLLEGE_NAME AS SPECIALTY_NAME "
+ " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP T LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON
C.COLLEGE_CODE=T.COLLEGE_CODE WHERE T.DATA_STATUS=? ";
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
planSql +=" AND T.PLAN_TYPE ='1' ";
jobsSql +=" AND T.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
planSql +=" AND T.PLAN_TYPE ='2' ";
jobsSql +=" AND T.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
}
planSql +=" ORDER BY T.PLAN_NAME DESC ";
jobsSql +=" ORDER BY C.COLLEGE_NAME DESC ";
List<HashMap> planList = DBQuery.sqlQuery(session,planSql, "1");
List<HashMap> depList = DBQuery.sqlQuery(session,jobsSql, "1");
List<HashMap> infoList = DBQuery.sqlQuery(session,"SELECT T.DEP_UID AS
SPECIALTY_CODE, T.JOB_UID AS CLASS_CODE, T.JOB_NAME AS CLASS_NAME FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO T WHERE T.JOB_STATUS=? ORDER BY T.JOB_NAME DESC", "1");
if(planList!=null&&planList.size()>0) {
dicList=new ArrayList<HashMap>();
Iterator<HashMap> it = planList.iterator();
while(it.hasNext()){
HashMap temMap = it.next();
HashMap collegeMap=new HashMap();
collegeMap.put("id", temMap.getString("PLAN_UID"));
collegeMap.put("name", temMap.getString("PLAN_NAME"));
List<HashMap> children =
EasydicDataUtil.getOneChilrenList(collegeMap.getString("id"),depList,infoList);
if(children!=null && children.size()>0) {
collegeMap.put("children", children);
}
dicList.add(collegeMap);
}
// CacheHolderString.setData(CacheHolderString.DIC_LIST_JOBSINFO, dicList);
}
return dicList;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.workstudy.util;
import java.util.List;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.ISession;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.Validate;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.db.DBQuery;
import com.easy.entity.workstudy.WorkstudyJobsInfo;
public class JobsValidateUtils {
/**
* 同年度 同类型的岗位计划是否存在
* */
public static boolean planIsEx(ISession session,String yearNum,String planType,String
planUid){
boolean isExist=false;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(planUid)){
String sql="SELECT F.PLAN_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN F WHERE
F.YEAR_NUM=? AND F.PLAN_TYPE=? AND F.PLAN_UID!=? AND F.PLAN_STATUS!='-1' ";
List<?> tempList=DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, sql, yearNum, planType, planUid);
if(tempList!=null&&tempList.size()>0){
isExist=true;
}
}else{
String sql="SELECT F.PLAN_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN F WHERE
F.YEAR_NUM=? AND F.PLAN_TYPE=? AND F.PLAN_STATUS!='-1' ";
List<?> tempList=DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, sql, yearNum, planType);
if(tempList!=null&&tempList.size()>0){
isExist=true;
}
}
return isExist;
}
/**
* 岗位名称是否存在
* */
public static boolean jobNameIsEx(ISession session,String jobName,String jobUid,String
depUid){
boolean isExist=false;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(jobUid)){
String sql="SELECT F.JOB_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO F WHERE
F.JOB_NAME=? AND F.JOB_UID!=? AND F.DEP_UID=? ";
List<?> tempList=DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, sql, jobName,jobUid,depUid);
if(tempList!=null&&tempList.size()>0){
isExist=true;
}
}else{
String sql="SELECT F.JOB_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO F WHERE
F.JOB_NAME=? AND F.DEP_UID=? ";
List<?> tempList=DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, sql, jobName,depUid);
if(tempList!=null&&tempList.size()>0){
isExist=true;
}
}
return isExist;
}
/**
* 学生是否在同一岗位重复上岗
* */
public static boolean jobEmployIsEx(ISession session,String stuNo,String employUid,String
jobUid){
boolean isExist=false;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(jobUid)){
String sql="SELECT F.EMPLOY_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY F WHERE
F.JOB_UID=? AND F.STU_NO=? AND F.EMPLOY_UID!=? ";
List<?> tempList=DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, sql, jobUid,stuNo,employUid);
if(tempList!=null&&tempList.size()>0){
isExist=true;
}
}else{
String sql="SELECT F.EMPLOY_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY F WHERE
F.JOB_UID=? AND F.STU_NO=? ";
List<?> tempList=DBQuery.sqlQuery(session, sql, jobUid,stuNo);
if(tempList!=null&&tempList.size()>0){
isExist=true;
}
}
return isExist;
}
public static boolean vaildateNum(ISession session, WorkstudyJobsInfo info,String
employUid){
boolean isExist=false;
String sql="SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT F.STU_NO) FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY F
WHERE F.JOB_UID=? AND F.EMPLOY_STATUS=? AND F.EMPLOY_UID !=? ";
Integer num = DBQuery.queryForInteger(session, sql, info.getJobUid(),"1",employUid);
if("1".equals(info.getIsLimitNum()) && info.getNeedNum()>0 && num+1 >
info.getNeedNum()) {
isExist=true;
}
return isExist;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.workstudy;
import java.io.File;

@Plugin(
transcode = "jobsEmployManage", transname = "勤工助学岗位雇用", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-29"
)
@Transactional
public class JobsEmployManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String isE="0";//是否导出
String jobsSelvalue=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("JOBS_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
jobsSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(jobsSelvalue,null);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("PLAN_UID",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DEP_UID",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("JOB_UID",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"')
";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE",true));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE",true));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT",true));
formats.put("EMPLOY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("EMPLOY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_EMPLOY_STATUS"));
// formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("CREATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("CREATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("EMPLOY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("EMPLOY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("LEAVE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("LEAVE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
if(Validate.isEmpty(isE)|| "0".equals(isE)){
formats.put("CREATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("CREATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
}
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.EMPLOY_UID, T.JOB_UID, T.STU_NO, T.STU_TELEPHONE, T.EMPLOY_DATE, T.LEAVE_DATE, T.EMPLOY_STATUS, T.EMPLOY_REMARK, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE");
sqlBuild.append(" , T.CREATE_UID, T.CREATE_DATE, JI.JOB_NAME, JI.COLLEGE_CODE, JI.SALARY_AMOUNT, JI.SALARY_UNIT, JI.JOB_TYPE, JC.COLLEGE_NAME ,JD.PLAN_TYPE, JD.DEP_UID, JP.PLAN_NAME,JP.PLAN_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
sqlBuild.append(" ,CASE WHEN KNS.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS
");
}
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID
LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE JC ON JC.COLLEGE_CODE = JI.COLLEGE_CODE ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP JD ON JD.DEP_UID=JI.DEP_UID
LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN JP ON JP.PLAN_UID = JD.PLAN_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.STU_NO) AS
KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) KNS ON KNS.STU_NO = T.STU_NO ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.EMPLOY_STATUS!='-1' ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString() , arrayList.toArray());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
exportData(statisticsList, surestream);
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
String[] headers={"用工部门/学院","岗位名称","岗位计划","计划类别","岗
位类别","学号","姓名","所在学院"
,"是否困难生","联系电话","报酬标准" ,"是否在岗"};
String[]
column={"COLLEGE_NAME","JOB_NAME","PLAN_NAME","PLAN_TYPE","JOB_TYPE","STU_NO","S
TU_STU_NAME","STU_COLLEGE_NAME", "SFKNS","STU_TELEPHONE","SALARY_AMOUNT","EMPLOY_STATUS_SV"};
String title=" 岗 位 雇 佣 信 息
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String employUid = surestream.getString("employUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(employUid, "【ID】不能为空");
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, JI.JOB_NAME, JI.SALARY_AMOUNT, JI.SALARY_UNIT, JI.JOB_TYPE, JC.COLLEGE_NAME, JI.DEP_UID, D.PLAN_UID
");
if("1".equals(isView)) {
sqlBuild.append(" ,P.PLAN_NAME,P.YEAR_NUM,P.PLAN_TYPE , CASE WHEN
K.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS ");
}
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID
LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE JC ON JC.COLLEGE_CODE = JI.COLLEGE_CODE ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON D.DEP_UID=JI.DEP_UID ");
if("1".equals(isView)) {
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON
P.PLAN_UID=D.PLAN_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.APPLY_UID) AS
KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) K ON K.STU_NO=T.STU_NO ");
}
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.EMPLOY_UID =? ");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE"));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT"));
formats.put("EMPLOY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("EMPLOY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_EMPLOY_STATUS"));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK"));
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("EMPLOY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("EMPLOY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("LEAVE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("LEAVE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE"));
formats.put("CREATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("CREATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));
formats.put("CREATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("CREATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
HashMap employMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, employUid);
surestream.put("data", employMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String employUid = surestream.getString("EMPLOY_UID");//
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");//学号
// Date employDate = surestream.getDate("EMPLOY_DATE");//雇用日期
// Date leaveDate = surestream.getDate("LEAVE_DATE");//离岗日期
String bankName = surestream.getString("BANK_NAME");
String bankCode = surestream.getString("BANK_CODE");//银行账号
String setupSelvalue = surestream.getString("SETUP_SELVALUE");
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(setupSelvalue,null);
if(arrCode ==null || arrCode.length==0) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息 ID】不能为空");
}
String jobUid = arrCode[2];//岗位 id
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(jobUid, "【岗位 id】不能为空");
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo==null || Validate.isEmpty(studentInfo.getStuNo())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息】不存在");
}
WorkstudyJobsInfo info = this.get(WorkstudyJobsInfo.class, jobUid);
if (info == null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息】不存在");
}
if(JobsValidateUtils.jobEmployIsEx(getSession(), stuNo, employUid, info.getJobUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, " 【 "+stuNo+" 】 同 学 已 经 在
"+info.getJobName()+"岗位下被录用了！");
}
if(JobsValidateUtils.vaildateNum(getSession(), info, employUid)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位需求人数】已满足！");
}
try{
WorkstudyJobsEmploy employ = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(employUid)) {
employ = this.get(WorkstudyJobsEmploy.class, employUid);
}
//填充值
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(employ)&&!Validate.isEmpty(employ.getEmployUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), employ);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(employ.getEmployStatus())) {
employ.setEmployStatus("1");
}
employ.setJobUid(info.getJobUid());
employ.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
employ.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
employ.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
employ.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(employ);
} else {
employ = new WorkstudyJobsEmploy();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), employ);
employUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyemployuid");
employ.setJobUid(info.getJobUid());
employ.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
employ.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
employ.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
employ.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
employ.setEmployUid(employUid);
employ.setEmployStatus("1");
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
employ.setCreateDate(nowDate);
employ.setCreateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(employ);
}
//更新
studentInfo.setTelNum(employ.getStuTelephone());//电话号码
if(!Validate.isEmpty(bankCode)) {
studentInfo.setBankCode(bankCode);//银行账号
studentInfo.setBankName(bankName);
}
this.update(studentInfo);
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String employUids = surestream.getString("employUids");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(employUids, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
String leaveDateStr = surestream.getString("LEAVE_DATE");
String employRemark = surestream.getString("EMPLOY_REMARK");
Date leaveDate = null;
if("0".equals(dataStatus)) {
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(leaveDateStr, "【离岗日期】不能为空");
leaveDate = DateUtil.strToDate(leaveDateStr);
}
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, employUids.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
Date nowDate = DateSource.getTradedate();
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
WorkstudyJobsEmploy employ = this.get(WorkstudyJobsEmploy.class, id);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(employ)&&!Validate.isEmpty(employ.getEmployUid())){
employ.setEmployStatus(dataStatus);
if("0".equals(dataStatus)) {
employ.setLeaveDate(leaveDate);
}
if("1".equals(dataStatus)) {
employ.setEmployDate(nowDate);
employ.setLeaveDate(null);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(employRemark)) {
if(!Validate.isEmpty(employ.getEmployRemark())) {
employ.setEmployRemark(employ.getEmployRemark()+"//"+employRemark);
}else {
employ.setEmployRemark(employRemark);
}
}
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optUid);
this.update(employ);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【勤工助学岗位雇用】不存在");
}
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 批量删除
* id 以逗号,拼接
* **/
@Route
public boolean delete(ESurestream surestream) {
String employUid = surestream.getString("employUid");
try{
if (!Validate.isEmpty(employUid)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, employUid.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
//判断为空
if(!Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
this.update("UPDATE WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY SET
EMPLOY_STATUS=?, UPDATE_UID=? ,UPDATE_DATE=SYSDATE WHERE EMPLOY_UID=? AND
EMPLOY_STATUS = ? ", DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,optUid,id,"0");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
//@composite
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "删除成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 名单导入
* */
@Route
public boolean importExcel(ESurestream surestream) {
HttpServletRequest request=surestream.request();
// HttpServletResponse response=ResponseUtils.getResponse(surestream);
// if (!ServletFileUpload.isMultipartContent(request)) {
// throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897, "Request is not multipart, please
'multipart/form-data' enctype for your form" );
// }
try{
MultipartHttpServletRequest fileRequest = (MultipartHttpServletRequest)request;
for (Iterator<?> it = fileRequest.getFileNames(); it.hasNext();) {
String key = (String) it.next();
MultipartFile multipartFile = fileRequest.getFile(key);
String
filesuffix=UEditorConfigUitl.getFileSuffix(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename());//获取上传文件的
后缀名
if(!".xlsx".equals(filesuffix.toLowerCase())){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,"[非.xlsx]类型文件不允许上传");
}
InputStream fileIS = multipartFile.getInputStream();
String excelname = multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().substring(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().indexOf("."));
//得到部署路径
// String rootPath =
SingletonService.getRealPath().replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separator")).replace("\\", System.getProperty("file.separator"));
// excel 列结构
List<ExcelColumn> excelColumns = new ArrayList<ExcelColumn>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(0, "COLLEGE_NAME", "用工部门/学院
"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(1, "JOB_NAME", "岗位名称"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(2, "PLAN_NAME", "岗位计划"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(3, "XH", "学号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(4, "XM", "姓名"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(5, "YHZH", "中国银行帐号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(6, "YHZHKHH", "银行开户行"));
ExcelHead head = new ExcelHead();
head.setRowCount(1); // 头所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
try {
stuList = ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().importToObjectList(head, multipartFile.getInputStream());
} catch (Exception e) {
throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897,"导入岗位雇用信息失败" );
}
String stuNo = null;//学号
String stuName = null;//姓名
String collegeName = null;//
String jobName = null;//
String planName = null;//
String yhzh=null,yhzhkhh=null;
int countAdd = 0 ; //新增条数
//int countUpdate = 0;//更新条数
int failcnt = 0;//导入失败计数
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String remark = "";
for(HashMap stuMap : stuList){
remark = "";
int errcnt = 0;
//学号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XH"))){
stuNo = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XH").trim());
}else{
remark +="学号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//姓名
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XM"))){
stuName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XM").trim());
}else{
remark +="姓名不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//用工部门/学院
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME"))){
collegeName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="用工部门/学院不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//岗位名称
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("JOB_NAME"))){
jobName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("JOB_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="岗位名称不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//计划名称
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("PLAN_NAME"))){
planName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("PLAN_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="计划名称不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//中国银行卡号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("YHZH"))){
yhzh = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("YHZH").trim());
}else{
remark +="中国银行卡号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//开户行
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("YHZHKHH"))){
yhzhkhh = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("YHZHKHH").trim());
yhzhkhh = CacheHolderDicTree.getCodeByName("SYS_DM_BANK",yhzhkhh);
if(Validate.isEmpty(yhzhkhh)) {
remark +="开户行字典数据不存在！";
errcnt++;
}
}else{
remark +="开户行不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
HashMap jobMap = null;
HashMap planMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT PLAN_UID,PLAN_TYPE
FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P WHERE P.PLAN_NAME=? AND P.PLAN_STATUS='1' ", planName);
if(planMap != null) {
HashMap depMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
D.DEP_UID,D.COLLEGE_CODE FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C
ON C.COLLEGE_CODE = D.COLLEGE_CODE WHERE D.PLAN_UID=? AND C.COLLEGE_NAME=?
AND D.DATA_STATUS=? ", planMap.getString("PLAN_UID"),collegeName,"1");
if(depMap!=null) {
jobMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
JI.JOB_UID,JI.COLLEGE_CODE FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI WHERE JI.JOB_NAME=? AND
JI.DEP_UID=? AND JI.JOB_STATUS = ? ", jobName, depMap.getString("DEP_UID"),"1");
if(jobMap!=null
&& !Validate.isEmpty(jobMap.getString("JOB_UID"))) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT EMPLOY_UID FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY P WHERE P.JOB_UID=? AND P.STU_NO=? AND
P.EMPLOY_STATUS!='-1' ", jobMap.getString("JOB_UID"), stuNo)) {
remark +="【" + stuNo + "】 学号的学生已经在【"+
jobName +"】岗位上.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 部门/学院的【"+
jobName +"】岗位信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + planName + "】计划中该部门或学院的信息
不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + planName + "】计划的信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
// if(!this.existSQL("SELECT PLAN_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P
WHERE P.PLAN_NAME=? AND P.PLAN_STATUS='1' ", planName)) {
// remark +="【" + planName + "】计划的信息不存在或未启用.";
// errcnt++;
// }
//效验学号和姓名是否一致
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo!=null) {
if(!stuName.equals(studentInfo.getStuName())) {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】和姓名【"+ stuName +"】对
应的学生不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】的学生信息不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
if(jobMap==null) {
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 部门/学院的【"+ jobName +"】
岗位信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
//没错就进行保存操作
if(errcnt==0) {
try{
WorkstudyJobsEmploy employ = new WorkstudyJobsEmploy();
employ.setEmployUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyemployuid"));
// employ.setEmployDate(employDate);
// employ.setLeaveDate(leaveDate);
employ.setEmployRemark("导入数据");
employ.setEmployStatus("1");
employ.setJobUid(jobMap.getString("JOB_UID"));
employ.setStuNo(stuNo);
employ.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
employ.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
employ.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
employ.setStuTelephone(studentInfo.getTelNum());
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
employ.setCreateDate(nowDate);
employ.setCreateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(employ);
//更新学生银行卡信息
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yhzh)){
studentInfo.setBankName(yhzhkhh);
studentInfo.setBankCode(yhzh);
this.update(studentInfo);
}
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]导入成功.";
countAdd++;
}catch (Exception e) {
failcnt++;
}
}else {
failcnt++;
}
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", remark);
}
String rootPath = Configurations.instance().getString("easy.upload.file.path").replace("/",System.getProperty("file.s
eparator"));
//生成处理结果文件
String zdypath = DicConst.IMPWORKSTUDY_PATH+File.separator;
String excelpath = rootPath + zdypath;;
File fDbfpath =new File(excelpath);
//如果文件夹不存在则创建
if (!fDbfpath.exists() && !fDbfpath.isDirectory()){
Logs.log().info( "[" + excelpath + "]不存在,创建" );
fDbfpath .mkdir();
}
String wdbffilename = DicConst.IMPWORKSTUDY_PATH+"_GWGY_" +
DateSource.getTradedate(CFrame.DatePattern5 ) + excelname;
String wdbffilepath = excelpath + wdbffilename;
String cdbffilepath = zdypath + wdbffilename;
File outputFile = new File(wdbffilepath);
// 需要特殊转换的单元
//Map<String, Map> headMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Map>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(excelColumns.size(), "IMPREMARK", "导
入提示备注"));
head.setRowCount(1); // 模板中头部所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().exportExcelFile(head, fileIS, outputFile, stuList);
//返回数据
surestream.put("resultinfo", " 导 入 岗 位 雇 用 信 息 处 理 结 果 , 成 功 [" +
countAdd +"]条,失败["+ failcnt +"]条请下载处理结果文件" );
surestream.put("retfilename", wdbffilename);//处理结果文件名
surestream.put("retfilepath", cdbffilepath);//处理结果文件存放路径
}
} catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "导入操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
}
